            <div id="vxstream-warnings" class="signature-details collapse in">
                                    <li class="list-group-item wraparound">Enforcing malicious verdict, as a reliable source indicates high confidence</li>
                                    <li class="list-group-item wraparound">The analysis system failed to start the input sample. Error code: 193 (ERROR_BAD_EXE_FORMAT)</li>
                            </div>
        </ul>
    
        </section>
